        event.preventDefault();
        var target = $(this).data("target");
        var targetElement = document.getElementById(target);

        targetElement.scrollIntoView({ behavior: "smooth" });

        setTimeout(function () {
          $("#" + target)
            .siblings(".expandable-content")
            .slideDown();
